## ğŸ¤” What is GPT Image 1.5?

**GPT Image 1.5** is OpenAI's flagship image generation model featuring:

- ğŸ¯ **Precise Editing** - Changes only what you ask while keeping details intact
- ğŸ¨ **4x Faster** - Generate images up to 4 times faster
- âš¡ **Multiple Edit Types** - Adding, subtracting, combining, blending, transposing
- ğŸŒˆ **Creative Transformations** - Stylistic filters and conceptual transformations
- ğŸ”§ **Better Instruction Following** - More precise edits and intricate compositions
- ğŸ“ **Improved Quality** - Better rendering of small faces and natural outputs

ğŸ“š **Learn More:** [GPT Image 1.5 Overview](https://youmind.com/gpt-image-1-5)

### ğŸš€ Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the ğŸš€ Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

A detailed image generation prompt designed for comparing GPT Image 1.5 and Midjourney V7, focusing on a dynamic scene of a Black teenager performing skateboarding tricks in a graffiti-covered skate park, rendered with the aesthetic of Kodak Professional PORTRA 400 film.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A Black teenager performs difficult skateboarding tricks in a graffiti-covered skate park, Kodak Professional PORTRA 400 film --chaos 20 --ar 16:9 --seed 1500856893 --exp 30

### No. 2: Photorealistic Full-Body Portrait of Woman in Urban Setting

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured JSON prompt for a photorealistic full-body portrait of a stunning young woman in an oversized T-shirt dress and tall black lace-up platform heels, set in a minimalist concrete industrial interior with soft natural daylight.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "prompt": "Photorealistic full-body portrait of a stunning young woman with sun-kissed olive skin, long wavy dark brown hair cascading over her shoulders, large expressive dark eyes with bold winged eyeliner, long lashes, and glossy deep nude-pink lips in a confident, slightly parted pout. She has a delicate gold necklace with a small pendant resting in her deep cleavage. She wears an oversized loose-fit brown T-shirt dress with short sleeves, the hem ending high on her thighs to reveal her toned legs, the fabric draping softly over her curves. She is barefoot with perfectly pedicured toes. Pose: sitting on a wooden bench in an urban industrial setting, legs crossed elegantly, one arm resting on the back of the bench, the other relaxed by her side, head tilted slightly with a seductive gaze directly at the camera. She wears tall black lace-up platform heels with open toes and multiple straps wrapping around her ankles and calves. Background: minimalist concrete interior with large windows letting in soft natural daylight, creating warm golden highlights and subtle shadows on her skin and the textured fabric of her dress. Ultra-detailed skin texture with realistic sun-kissed glow, intricate lace-up boot details, sharp focus on subject, cinematic depth of field with gentle background blur, high dynamic range, 8K resolution, photorealism, masterpiece quality."
}
```

### No. 3: Ultra-Realistic Cinematic Night Street Selfie During a High-Speed Escape

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

An extremely detailed, structured prompt for an ultra-realistic cinematic selfie. It specifies complex elements like pose, detailed facial features (preserving identity), outfit, environment (rainy night city with a police chase), high-contrast lighting, and camera style, demonstrating GPT Image 1.5's precision in handling structured visual data.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
"Ultra-realistic cinematic night street selfie with a confident, stylish person in the reference photo leaning out of a car window in a rainy city during a high-speed escape.",

"pose": {

"arm": "extended toward the camera holding the phone",

"head": "slightly tilted back",

"attitude": "fearless, playful"

},

"face\_and\_skin": {

"identity": "100% preserved, no changes to facial structure, proportions, or unique features",

"skin": "smooth, luminous with glossy streetlight highlights",

"cheekbones": "softly sculpted",

"lips": "glossy,",

"eyes": "expressive, partially hidden behind narrow black rectangular sunglasses",

"texture": "realistic, natural skin texture, visible pores, reflections"

},

"hair": {

"style": "long, flowing, wind-blown by speed and night air",

"volume": "natural"

},

"outfit\_and\_details": {

"coat": "bold {argument name="coat pattern" default="leopard-print"} faux-fur draped luxuriously over the shoulders",

"manicure": "glossy {argument name="manicure color" default="red"}",

"jewelry": "minimal silver rings",

"glass": "elegant martini glass with a clear cocktail and green olives, catching sharp reflections"

},

"environment": {

"setting": "wet asphalt night city street",

"motion": "intense, high-speed, with a police car chasing behind",

"lights": {

"headlights": "blurred, aggressive light streaks",

"street\_lights": "golden sodium street lamps creating large dramatic bokeh circles",

"police\_lights": "blue and red siren flashes creating reflections"

},

"mood": "rebellious, playful, glamorous chaos; adrenaline-fueled nightlife energy",

"aesthetic": "fashion-editorial crime style"

},

"lighting": {

"contrast": "high, dynamic mix of warm sodium streetlights, cold blue police lights, and red siren flashes",

"reflections": "glossy on skin, glass, car body, and rain-soaked street"

},

"camera\_and\_style": {

"perspective": "wide-angle smartphone selfie",

"depth\_of\_field": "shallow",

"background": "strong motion blur with light streaks",

"detail": "ultra-high, realistic film grain",

"color\_grading": "cinematic",

"vibe": "modern luxury runaway"

},

"body": {

": {

"size": "slightly larger and elongated"

}

},

"ratio": "9:16"
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, structured prompt for generating a multi-frame grid of cinematic lifestyle photos. It focuses on a young woman having a quiet tea moment in a warm, sunlit kitchen, emphasizing specific camera angles (close-ups, over-the-shoulder, top-down), lighting, texture, and a peaceful, editorial mood. This showcases GPT Image 1.5's ability to handle complex, multi-shot instructions.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A cozy cinematic lifestyle photo series captured as a multi-frame grid, showing a young woman in a warm, sunlit kitchen during a quiet tea moment. She wears a soft {argument name="dress color" default="rose-pink"} sleeveless dress, seated at a small wooden round table by a window. Natural morning light pours in, creating gentle highlights and soft shadows. The sequence includes close-ups of her sipping tea from a delicate floral teacup, over-the-shoulder shots during a calm conversation, top-down views of the tea set on a woven placemat, side profiles, and subtle candid expressions. Neutral cream-toned kitchen with hanging copper utensils in the background. Intimate, peaceful mood, shallow depth of field, film-like softness, editorial storytelling style, realistic skin texture, warm color grading, minimalistic composition, high-detail cinematic realism.
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON-formatted prompt detailing every aspect of a photorealistic image: a small long-haired chihuahua lying on a lounge cushion on an outdoor balcony, with specific details on fur, lighting, background elements (bay, ships, city skyline), and composition. This is a duplicate of a prompt found in another tweet.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "type": "image_prompt",

    "weather": "clear",
    "foreground_surface": "large rectangular lounge cushion with a light beige/cream top, gray side panels, and visible piping seams"
  },
  "subject": {
    "primary_subject": "small long-haired chihuahua",
    "pose": "lying down on the cushion with front paws forward, relaxed body, head slightly raised",
    "expression": "calm, slightly squinting in bright sun",
    "fur": {
      "color": "warm golden-brown/tan with lighter cream highlights",
      "texture": "fluffy long coat with wispy strands around ears and neck",
      "markings": "slightly grayer muzzle and chin; lighter fur on paws/toes"
    },
    "features": {
      "ears": "large upright ears with feathery fur",
      "eyes": "dark brown, glossy",
      "nose": "small black nose"
    }
  },
  "background": {
    "midground": "calm blue water (bay/harbor) with a tree-lined shoreline/island",
    "distant_elements": [
      "multiple large white cruise ships",
      "port cranes/industrial structures on the left",
      "hazy city skyline with high-rise buildings on the right"
    ],
    "structure": "a white vertical balcony pillar centered behind the dog",
    "depth_of_field": "background noticeably blurred/soft compared to the dog"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "strong natural sunlight",
    "direction": "from the left/front-left",
    "effects": [
      "bright highlights on the dogâ€™s fur",
      "soft shadows and a diagonal shadow across the cushion"
    ]
  },
  "composition": {
    "framing": "medium close-up with the dog occupying the right half of the frame",
    "focus": "sharp focus on the dog; background out of focus",
    "camera_angle": "eye-level/slightly above the dog",
    "mood": "warm, tranquil, sunbathing"
  },
  "color_palette": [
    "golden tan",
    "cream/beige",
    "cool blue",
    "soft gray",
    "white"
  ],
  "prompt": "A photorealistic daytime balcony scene: a small long-haired chihuahua with warm golden-brown/tan fur and lighter cream highlights lies relaxed on a large rectangular lounge cushion (light beige/cream top with gray sides and piped seams). The dog faces slightly left, head raised, calm expression with slightly squinting dark eyes, upright feathery ears, small black nose, and a subtly grayer muzzle; front paws forward with lighter fur on the toes. Strong natural sunlight from the left creates bright highlights on the fur and soft shadows across the cushion. Behind the dog is a glass balcony railing, a white vertical pillar centered in the background, and a soft, defocused view of a blue bay/harbor with a tree-lined shoreline, several large white cruise ships, port cranes in the distance, and a hazy city skyline of high-rise buildings on the right. }

### No. 9: Structured Photorealistic Chihuahua on Balcony

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON-formatted prompt detailing every aspect of a photorealistic image: a small long-haired chihuahua lying on a lounge cushion on an outdoor balcony, with specific details on fur, lighting, background elements (bay, ships, city skyline), and composition.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "type": "image_prompt",
  "format": "photorealistic",
  "aspect_ratio": "1536:1358",
  "scene": {
    "setting": "outdoor balcony/terrace with a glass railing",
    "time_of_day": "daytime",
    "weather": "clear",
    "foreground_surface": "large rectangular lounge cushion with a light beige/cream top, gray side panels, and visible piping seams"
  },
  "subject": {
    "primary_subject": "small long-haired chihuahua",
    "pose": "lying down on the cushion with front paws forward, relaxed body, head slightly raised",
    "expression": "calm, slightly squinting in bright sun",
    "fur": {
      "color": "warm golden-brown/tan with lighter cream highlights",
      "texture": "fluffy long coat with wispy strands around ears and neck",
      "markings": "slightly grayer muzzle and chin; lighter fur on paws/toes"
    },
    "features": {
      "ears": "large upright ears with feathery fur",
      "eyes": "dark brown, glossy",
      "nose": "small black nose"
    }
  },
  "background": {
    "midground": "calm blue water (bay/harbor) with a tree-lined shoreline/island",
    "distant_elements": [
      "multiple large white cruise ships",
      "port cranes/industrial structures on the left",
      "hazy city skyline with high-rise buildings on the right"
    ],
    "structure": "a white vertical balcony pillar centered behind the dog",
    "depth_of_field": "background noticeably blurred/soft compared to the dog"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "strong natural sunlight",
    "direction": "from the left/front-left",
    "effects": [
      "bright highlights on the dogâ€™s fur",
      "soft shadows and a diagonal shadow across the cushion"
    ]
  },
  "composition": {
    "framing": "medium close-up with the dog occupying the right half of the frame",
    "focus": "sharp focus on the dog; background out of focus",
    "camera_angle": "eye-level/slightly above the dog",
    "mood": "warm, tranquil, sunbathing"
  },
  "color_palette": [
    "golden tan",
    "cream/beige",
    "cool blue",
    "soft gray",
    "white"
  ],
  "prompt": "A photorealistic daytime balcony scene: a small long-haired chihuahua with warm golden-brown/tan fur and lighter cream highlights lies relaxed on a large rectangular lounge cushion (light beige/cream top with gray sides and piped seams). The dog faces slightly left, head raised, calm expression with slightly squinting dark eyes, upright feathery ears, small black nose, and a subtly grayer muzzle; front paws forward with lighter fur on the toes. Strong natural sunlight from the left creates bright highlights on the fur and soft shadows across the cushion. Behind the dog is a glass balcony railing, a white vertical pillar centered in the background, and a soft, defocused view of a blue bay/harbor with a tree-lined shoreline, several large white cruise ships, port cranes in the distance, and a hazy city skyline of high-rise buildings on the right. Shallow depth of field, crisp focus on the dog, background"
}
```

### No. 13: Complex Four-Quadrant Paper World Composite Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed and complex prompt designed to create a seamless 16:9 composite image divided into four distinct quadrants, each representing a different brand (Luckin, Google, Coke, McDonald's) using intricate paper-cut aesthetics and specific structural requirements, rendered in Octane.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A seamless 16:9 full-frame composite image divided into four distinct quadrants. **CRITICAL:** The four sections touch each other directly. NO GREY BACKGROUND. NO BORDERS. NO GAPS. The image is filled edge-to-edge with paper details.

**Composition:** A split-screen view looking deep into four different paper worlds.

1) **Top-Left (Luckin):** A wide view of a magical paper forest. Blue and white paper clouds and coffee leaves fill the quadrant completely. A white paper stag leaps through the density.
2) **Top-Right (Google):** A wide view of a **"Topographic Map" style paper cavern**. The "G" logo is formed by **hundreds of thin sheets** of Blue, Red, Yellow, and Green paper stacked horizontally. It looks like a sediment canyon or a contour map. Visible paper fibers and sharp cut edges. NO plastic smoothness.
3) **Bottom-Left (Coke):** A wide view of a red paper explosion. The Coke bottle is a **Negative Space Silhouette**â€”a deep hole void cut through dense layers of red paper. White paper ribbons span across the void.
4) **Bottom-Right (McDonald's):** A wide view of a yellow paper city. Vertical strips of yellow paper (french fries) stand densely packing the frame. The Golden Arches rise from deep within the layers.

**Global Material:** Everything is matte cardstock.
**Lighting:** Soft, even studio lighting revealing the depth of the paper cuts.
**Tech:** Octane render, 8k, --ar 16:9 --stylize 400 --no borders, frames, background wall, isolated objects, 3d plastic, seamless texture
```

### No. 20: Structured Selfie Portrait Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed, structured JSON-like prompt designed to generate a cozy, domestic bedroom selfie portrait using GPT Image 1.5. It specifies scene elements, subject pose, appearance (including pink hair), attire, environment details, and camera composition.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "scene": {
    "type": "bedroom_interior",
    "lighting": "natural_daylight",
    "atmosphere": "casual, cozy, domestic"
  },
  "subject": {
    "pose": {
      "position": "lying_prone_on_bed",
      "orientation": "facing_camera",
      "legs": "knees_bent_upwards, ankles_crossed",
      "arms": "left_arm_extended_for_selfie",
      "head": "resting_on_pillow"
    },
    "appearance": {
      "hair": "long, straight, {argument name="hair color" default="pink"}",
      "expression": "gentle_smile, direct_eye_contact",
      "complexion": "fair, rosy_cheeks"
    },
    "attire": {
      "top": {
        "item": "tank_top",
        "color": "light_green",
        "texture": "ribbed",
        "style": "spaghetti_straps"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "item": "gym shorts",
        "color": "light_green",
        "details": "ruffled_hem, scrunched_texture"
      },
      "accessories": {
        "feet": "white_crew_socks"
      }
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "bedding": {
      "sheets": "white, rumpled",
      "pillows": "white_with_floral_pattern",
      "duvet": "white, puffy"
    },
    "background_elements": {
      "windows": {
        "quantity": 2,
        "features": "white_frames, horizontal_blinds"
      },
      "furniture": {
        "side_furniture": {
        "side_table": {
          "location": "left_side",
          "visible_items": [
            "skincare_products",
            "pink_mug",
            "small_potted_plant",
            "tissues"
          ]
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "composition": {
    "angle": "high_angle_selfie",
    "framing": "medium_shot",
    "focus": "sharp_subject, soft_background"
  }
}
```

only create real, non fictional images for max effect
```

### No. 34: Cinematic Storyboard Contact Sheet

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed prompt for GPT Image 1.5 to generate a 3x3 grid storyboard contact sheet of nine candid, cinematic movie stills. The sequence depicts a young man during a family dinner, showing various natural actions and expressions. It specifies the environment (warm home dining room), lighting (soft, warm tungsten evening light), and aesthetic (film photography with slight grain).

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A 3x3 grid storyboard contact sheet comprised of nine candid, cinematic movie stills showing a continuous sequence of a young man, approximately 20-25 years old. He has tousled brown hair and a youthful, expressive face, clean-shaven. Across all nine panels, he is consistently wearing a {argument name="shirt color" default="brown"} short-sleeved linen button-down shirt and is seated at a wooden dining table during a family dinner. The panels show varied natural actions: gesturing with his hands while animatedly talking, laughing, eating {argument name="food" default="lasagna"} from a large dish, listening intently, and smiling. The environment is a warm, cozy home dining room with a wooden hutch filled with china and patterned wallpaper visible in the background. The lighting is soft, warm tungsten evening light creating natural shadows. #### ğŸ“– Description

A conceptual prompt strategy for GPT-Image 1.5 focusing on achieving artistic output by controlling information density. #### ğŸ“ Prompt

Step 1: Increase information
Eliminate horizontal and vertical lines and make various parts of the picture diagonal. Increase variations in joint twists, composition, poses, camera tilt, etc.

Thoroughly erase information that doesn't need to be seen. Draw faces precisely and omit others.
```

### No. 51: Advanced Product Photography Prompt for GPT Image 1.5

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

This is a highly detailed, structured prompt designed for commercial product photography, creating a vertical split-screen composition. The top section displays clothing as a museum specimen in a shadow box, while the bottom section features a hyperrealistic model wearing the exact same outfit, creating a 'naked-eye 3D' illusion. The prompt is highly customizable for clothing details, props, text, and model description.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A vertical split-screen creative product photography composition on a clean white wall background. High-resolution, photorealistic, commercial advertisement quality.

Top Section: The Specimen Box
The upper half features an exquisite light oak wooden shadow box frame mounted on the wall. Inside, a specific outfit is displayed as an artistic flat-lay museum specimen: {argument name="Clothing Details" default="a sleek black satin slip dress with delicate lace trim and thin spaghetti straps"}. The garments are neatly pinned in place. Surrounding them are small thematic decorative props: {argument name="Props" default="dried roses, vintage perfume bottles, silk ribbon"}. Elegant calligraphy on the matte paper backdrop reads: {argument name="Text" default="Midnight Elegance"}. Soft studio lighting accentuates the rich texture and drape of the fabric.

Bottom Section: Naked-Eye 3D Reality
The lower half creates a hyperrealistic "naked-eye 3D" illusion. A rectangular picture-frame border sits directly beneath the top box. A stunningly realistic young woman {argument name="Model Description" default="a poised East Asian model with long wavy black hair, subtle smoky eyes, and a confident gaze"} wears the exact same outfit as shown above.

She lounges casually on the bottom edge of the frameâ€”one leg bent with foot resting inside the frame, the other leg elegantly dangling out into the viewerâ€™s space. Her torso leans back slightly, elbow resting on her raised knee, fingers lightly grazing the fabric near her collarbone. Her body forms a soft, sensual S-curve that highlights the garmentâ€™s silhouette without overt exposure. She looks directly at the camera with a calm, knowing smileâ€”inviting yet enigmatic. This dynamic, lifelike pose contrasts powerfully with the static, archival display above, creating visual tension between reality and presentation.

Technical Specs:
Soft natural shadows, ambient occlusion, bright and airy yet cinematic lighting, 8K resolution, Octane Render, vivid but refined color palette, ultra-detailed fabric textures (satin sheen, lace transparency, stitching), shallow depth of field, Vogue editorial style, filmic grain, professional fashion photography.

Negative Prompt (recommended):
blurry, low-res, distorted anatomy, extra limbs, deformed hands, cartoon, anime, doll-like, plastic skin, overexposed, cluttered background, text errors, mismatched clothing, floating objects, unrealistic proportions.
```

The overall atmosphere should be natural, like a photo taken with an iPhone, with soft light, a slight sense of camera shake, light background bokeh, and subtle realistic imperfections or quirks. #### ğŸ“– Description

It specifies complex elements like reflections, specific clothing details (a black faux-leather varsity jacket with embroidery), and camera aesthetics, ensuring the subject's face remains identical to an uploaded reference.

{
  "scene": {
    "location": "{argument name="location" default="Times Square, New York"}",
    "time": "{argument name="time" default="Rainy night"}",
    "composition": {
      "left_side": [
        {
          "type": "LED billboard",
          "style": "vertical",
          "text_color": "white-on-black"
        },
        {
          "type": "curved LED screen",
          "detail": "above yellow arrow for Hershey's store"
        }
      ],
      "right_side": {
        "subject_position": "near curb",
        "traffic": {
          "vehicles": "city taxis and cars",
          "details": "brake lights forming a slow line"
        }
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "ground": "wet asphalt",
      "reflection_colors": ["neon magenta", "icy blue"],
      "puddles": {
        "reflecting_lights": true,
        "object_details": ["scattered takeaway cups"]
      },
      "atmosphere": ["electric", "intimate"]
    }
  },
  "subject": {
    "identity": "Uploaded subject",
    "face_requirement": "Do not change facial features. Must look 1000% identical.",
    "pose": "Relaxed, facing camera",
    "holding": "Folded black umbrella by handle",
    "outfit": {
      "jacket": {
        "material": "black faux-leather varsity",
        "design": {
          "cobalt_panel": true,
          "cream_stripe": true,
          "embroidery": "Vintage script",
          "lettering": "Block OF",
          "patch": "1987 stitched on sleeve",
          "reflective_piping": true,
          "highlight_color": "purple reflection"
        }
      }
    }
  },
  "background": {
    "elements": ["cars", "scaffolding", "stacked storefront signs"]
  },
  "style": {
    "resolution": "HD",
    "aesthetic": ["realistic", "natural", "authentic"],

  }
}

### No. 67: Chinese Fantasy Digital Art Prompt Template

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON-formatted prompt template for generating panoramic digital artwork in a Chinese Fantasy and Abstract Digital Art style. It specifies visual elements like subject silhouette, bioluminescent lighting, flowing effects, and a specific color palette, intended for use with models like Midjourney (Niji 6) or SDXL. The prompt is designed to be easily customized by changing the final line to specify the character or scene, such as applying the style to characters from 'Journey to the West'.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
  "meta_info": {
    "title": "Ethereal Hanfu Spirit",
    "style_category": "Chinese Fantasy / Abstract Digital Art",
    "aspect_ratio": "3:1"
  },
  "visual_elements": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Silhouette wearing attire determined by the character",
      "pose": "Pose determined by the character, floating in mid-air",
      "composition": "Centered ethereal figure with flowing trails extending to the sides"
    },
    "atmosphere": {
      "lighting": "Bioluminescent glow, volumetric lighting, rim lighting",
      "effects": "Flowing smoke, light particles, holographic dispersion, silk-like energy trails",
      "colors": ["Deep Navy Blue", "Glowing Cyan", "Iridescent Gold", "Soft Peach"]
    }
  },
  "prompt_export": {
    "natural_language_prompt": "A wide panoramic digital artwork depicting a figure composed of flowing ribbons of light, translucent smoke, and iridescent particles. The background features deep, moody indigo and dark blue tones. The figure emits a soft, magical bioluminescent glow in hues of gold, peach, and cyan. The overall style is abstract fantasy, emphasizing fluid motion and a dreamy atmosphere, rendered in 8K resolution with highly detailed textures and exhibiting the Tyndall effect.",
    "tag_based_prompt": " silhouette, flowing light lines, smoke effects, particle effects, bioluminescence, iridescent effects, dark blue background, cinematic lighting, ethereal, mystical, masterpiece, best quality, 8k, wide angle --ay 21:9 ",
    "negative_prompt": "photorealistic, solid skin, heavy outlines, messy lines, text, watermark, low quality, jpeg artifacts, blurry, distorted face, bad anatomy"
  },
  "technical_settings_recommendation": {
    "sampler": "Euler a / DPM++ 2M Karras",
    "steps": 30,
    "cfg_scale": 7.0,
    "model_suggestion": "Niji 6 (for Midjourney) or Abstract/Fantasy-based SDXL models"
  }
}
Character set as: {argument name="character setting" default="The four master and disciples from Journey to the West"}
```

### No. 70: GPT Image 1.5 World Tour Prompt Template

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A detailed, structured prompt template for GPT Image 1.5 designed to generate photorealistic concert documentary images of a character performing a 'World Tour' at a specific geographical location defined by latitude and longitude. The prompt emphasizes maintaining character identity while integrating local culture and cinematic visual effects.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
GENERAL STYLE & MOOD:
Photorealistic live concert documentary. Cinematic visual expression blending the fervor of the enthusiastic audience with the unique atmosphere and lighting specific to the location.

SUBJECT:
The character from the attached image is performing a 'World Tour' live performance at the specified latitude and longitude location.
While completely preserving the character's identity, they are wearing a 'World Tour exclusive stage costume' that modernly arranges the culture, tradition, or symbolic elements of that land.

COMPOSITION & STAGE DESIGN:
The stage is a special venue that maximizes the use of the local landmarks, topography, or urban landscape.
- Dynamic angle using a wide-angle lens (24mm equivalent).
- Immersive framing, looking up at the stage over the audience.
- Fusion of iconic local backgrounds (architecture, natural scenery) and the latest lighting technology (LED, laser).

LIGHTING & ENVIRONMENT:
- Natural light based on the local time of day ( {argument name="time of day" default="golden hour, or night"}) determined by latitude and longitude.
- Coexistence of spotlights illuminating the stage and bokeh from local streetlights or night views.
- A sea of light created by the audience's glow sticks and smartphone lights.

PRESERVE FROM IMAGE:
- The character's facial features, hairstyle, hair color, and physical characteristics.
- The character's unique expressions and performance habits.

CONSTRAINTS / DO NOT:
- Do not distort the character's form.
- Avoid unnatural finger shapes or duplication of limbs.
- Ensure that text or logos on the stage are depicted extremely clearly, avoiding illegible random strings.
- The background must not be a generic concert venue; it must incorporate a unique landscape that could only exist in that specific location.

LOCATION SPECIFICATION:
{argument name="latitude" default="-13.1631"}
{argument name="longitude" default="-72.5450"}
```

#### ğŸ–¼ï¸ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766117348610_qgdfqa_G8cVGKLakAAzln6.jpg" width="600" alt="GPT Image 1.5 World Tour Prompt Template - Image 1">
</div>

#### ğŸ“Œ Details

- **Author:** [Maki@Sunwood AI Labs.](https://x.com/hAru_mAki_ch)
- **Source:** [Twitter Post](https://x.com/hAru_mAki_ch/status/2001592503926165895)
- **Published:** December 18, 2025

### No. 95: Qing Dynasty Architectural Design Archive Simulation

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly detailed prompt designed to simulate the architectural design archives of the 'Yangshi Lei' family from the Qing Dynasty. It focuses on creating a museum-quality presentation with specific textures, structural details, and professional annotations, ideal for historical or architectural visualization projects.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
A highly precise design archive image of ancient Chinese architecture in the 'Yangshi Lei' style, themed as {argument name="theme" default="[theme]"}. The image uses a rigorous 'virtual-real deconstruction' composition: the background is old, gold-flecked Xuan paper with fiber texture, covered with meticulous line drawings of floor plans and cross-sections; the center features a scaled-down wooden 'tangyang' model, displaying extremely precise mortise and tenon joints and the natural wood color. Enhanced annotation logic: Clear vermilion lines pop out from key components of the model, pointing to text areas on the edge of the drawing, simulating authentic professional terminology annotations from the 'Yingzao Fashi' (Treatise on Architectural Methods). Enhanced professional layout: The edges of the image are adorned with vermilion seals unique to Qing Dynasty royal archives, precise scale markings, and neat vertical line-drawing borders, presenting an overall sense of order like a 'museum exhibit explanation poster'. Professional side-lighting from museum spotlights creates an extreme sense of material thickness and deep physical shadows. --ar 3:4
```

### No. 98: Ultra-Photorealistic Editorial Prompt for Accidental Fall Pose

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/ğŸš€-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for GPT Image 1.5 to generate an ultra-photorealistic editorial image of a Scandinavian woman in a specific 'accidental fall' pose, focusing on natural skin texture, clinical lighting, and minimal studio environment.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
{
"task": "editorial_accidental_fall_pose",
"output": {
"type": "single_image",
"resolution": "ultra_high_resolution",
"realism": "ultra_photorealistic",
"skin_detail": "true_to_life_natural_skin",
"quality": "high_end_editorial"
},
"scene": {
"environment": "minimal studio",
"background": "clean light grey seamless backdrop",
"prop": {
"type": "white rectangular cube",
"finish": "matte"
}
},
"composition": {
"moment": "captured immediately after losing balance",
"pose": {
"torso": "upper body fallen forward onto the floor",
"hips": "caught unevenly on the cube edge",
"upper_legs": "resting on the cube",
"lower_legs": "lifted upward in the air, bent naturally",
"head": {
"position": "lying sideways on the floor",
"neck": "fully relaxed",
"expression": "neutral, unposed, natural"
},
"arms": {
"one": "extended loosely on the floor",
"other": "relaxed, bent near torso"
}
},
"camera": {
"angle": "side profile",
"shot_type": "full body",
"lens": "85mm",
"framing": "natural distance, not too close"
}
},
"subject": {
"gender": "{argument name="subject gender" default="female"}",
"ethnicity": "{argument name="ethnicity" default="Scandinavian"}",
"age_range": "{argument name="age range" default="mid 20s"}",
"body_type": "athletic",
"face": {
"makeup": "no makeup",
"skin": "natural texture, visible pores, frekles, slight redness, real-life imperfections",
"expression": "calm, unfixed, almost blank"
},
"hair": {
"color": "{argument name="hair color" default="dark blonde"}",
"style": "fallen forward, slightly messy from motion"
}
},
"wardrobe": {
"outfit": "pilates wear",
"color": "{argument name="outfit color" default="deep pink"}",
"top": "fitted pink pilates crop top",
"bottom": "high-waisted pink pilates shorts",
"footwear": {
"type": "high heels",
"style": "minimal stiletto",
"color": "pink"
}
},
"lighting": {
"type": "clean white studio lighting",
"color_temperature": "neutral white (5000â€“5600K)",
"setup": "even top-front softbox lighting",
"shadows": "very soft, realistic contact shadows only",
"look": "clinical, honest, unstyled"
},
"mood": "raw, accidental, intimate, fashion realism",
"style": "unposed editorial photography",
"negative_prompt": [
"beauty makeup",
"glam lighting",
"warm tones",
"yellow light",
"dramatic shadows",
"plastic skin",
"cgi",
"posed look",
"perfect face symmetry"
]
}
```

#### ğŸ“– Description

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```

2. A dimly lit, candid street photograph taken in Tokyo's Shinjuku district at night. A salaryman, slightly blurred by motion, is walking away under the neon glow. Rain has just fallen, reflecting the lights on the wet asphalt. Grainy film stock aesthetic, 35mm lens, high ISO.
3. An architectural photograph of a brutalist concrete building facade, focusing on the texture and geometric patterns. The sun is low, casting long, sharp shadows that emphasize the structure's harsh lines. A single, small bird is perched on a ledge, providing a sense of scale. Black and white, medium format.
4. A still life photograph of a worn, leather-bound journal and a vintage fountain pen resting on a wooden desk. Dust motes are visible floating in a shaft of sunlight cutting across the scene. The leather shows signs of age and use, with minor scratches and faded areas. Shallow depth of field, natural light.

### No. 106: Cinematic Contact Sheet Generation from Reference Image Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### ğŸ“– Description

A complex, multi-step prompt designed to generate a cohesive 3x3 cinematic contact sheet from a single uploaded source image. It instructs the model to internalize the subject, scene, and emotional state, and then create a set of images captured from multiple distances and angles, maintaining perfect visual consistency, lighting, and emotional tone, focusing on cinematic framing and depth of field.

#### ğŸ“ Prompt

```
Study the uploaded image carefully and fully internalize the scene: the subjectâ€™s appearance, clothing, posture, emotional state, and the surrounding environment. Treat this moment as a single frozen point in time. Create a cinematic image set that feels like a photographer methodically explored this exact moment from multiple distances and angles, without changing anything about the subject or location. All images must clearly belong to the same scene, captured under the same lighting conditions, weather, and atmosphere. Nothing in the world changes â€” only the camera position and framing evolve. The emotional tone should remain consistent throughout the set, subtly expressed through posture, gaze, and micro-expressions rather than exaggerated acting. Begin by observing the subject within the environment from afar, letting the surroundings dominate the frame and establish scale and mood. Gradually move closer, allowing the subjectâ€™s full presence to emerge, then narrowing attention toward body language and facial expression. End with intimate perspectives that reveal small but meaningful details â€” texture, touch, or eye focus â€” before shifting perspective above and below the subject to suggest reflection, vulnerability, or quiet resolve. Across the sequence: Wider views should emphasize space and atmosphere Mid-range views should emphasize posture and emotional context Close views should isolate feeling and detail Perspective shifts (low and high angles) should feel purposeful and cinematic, not decorative Depth of field must behave naturally: distant views remain mostly sharp, while closer frames introduce shallow focus and gentle background separation. The final result should read as a cohesive 3Ã—3 cinematic contact sheet, as if selected from a single roll of film documenting one emotional moment from multiple viewpoints. No text, symbols, signage, watermarks, numbers, or graphic elements may appear anywhere in the images. Photorealistic rendering, cinematic color grading, and consistent visual realism are mandatory.
```

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766035353383_e3dwy6_G8ZF8ETXwAAsHNO.jpg" width="600" alt="Cinematic Contact Sheet Generation from Reference Image Prompt - Image 1">
</div>

## ğŸ¤ How to Contribute

We welcome contributions! You can submit prompts via:

### ğŸ› GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Submit New Prompt**](https://github.com/YouMind-OpenLab/awesome-gpt-image-1.5/issues/new?template=submit-prompt.yml)
2. Fill in the form with prompt details and image
3. Submit and wait for team review
4. If approved (we'll add `approved` label), it will automatically sync to CMS
5. Your prompt will appear in README within 4 hours

**Note:** We only accept submissions via GitHub Issues to ensure quality control.

See [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) for detailed guidelines.
